520→\n   521→  return child;\n   522→}\n   523→\n   524→ObjectDefineProperty(execFile, promisify.custom, {\n   525→  __proto__: null,\n   526→  enumerable: false,\n   527→  value: customPromiseExecFunction(execFile),\n   528→});\n   529→\n   530→function copyProcessEnvToEnv(env, name, optionEnv) {\n   531→  if (process.env[name] &&\n   532→      (!optionEnv ||\n   533→ 648→  // process.env.NODE_V8_COVERAGE always propagates, making it possible to\n   649→  // collect coverage for programs that spawn with white-listed environment.\n   650→  copyProcessEnvToEnv(env, the user's options object.\n   699→    __proto__: null,\n   700→    ...options,\n   701→    args,\n   702→    cwd,\n   703→    detached: !!options.detached,\n   704→    envPairs,\n   705→    file,\n 187→        handle: handle,\n   188→        readable: true,\n   189→        writable: true,\n   190→      });\n   191→\n   192→      // If the socket was created by net.Server we will track the stdioStringToArray(stdio, channel) {\n   238→  const options = [];\n   239→\n   240→  switch (stdio) {\n   241→    case 'ignore':\n   242→    case 'overlapped':\n   243→    case 'pipe': ChildProcess() {\n   255→  FunctionPrototypeCall(EventEmitter, this);\n   256→\n   257→  this._closesNeeded = 1;\n   258→  this._closesGot = 0;\n   259→  this.connected = false;\n   260→\n   261→   273→      this.exitCode = exitCode;\n   274→    }\n   275→\n   276→    if (this.stdin) {\n   277→      this.stdin.destroy();\n   278→    }\n   279→\n   280→    this._handle.close();\n   281→ 290→      err.spawnargs = ArrayPrototypeSlice(this.spawnargs, 1);\n   291→      this.emit('error', err);\n   292→    } else {\n   293→      this.emit('exit', this.exitCode, this.signalCode);\n   294→    }\n   295→\n   296→    // If any of the stdio streams have not been touched,\n   297→    // then pull all the data through so that it can get the\n   298→    // eof and emit a 'close' event.\n   299→    // Do it on nextTick so that the user has one last chance\n   300→    // to consume the output, if for example they only want to\n   301→    // start reading the data once the process exits.\n   302→    process.nextTick(flushStdio, this);\n   303→\n   304→    maybeClose(this);\n   305→  };\n   306→  if (childProcessChannel.hasSubscribers) {\n   307→    childProcessChannel.publish({\n   308→      process: this,\n   309→    });\n   310→  }\n   311→}\n   312→ObjectSetPrototypeOf(ChildProcess.prototype, EventEmitter.prototype);\n   313→ObjectSetPrototypeOf(ChildProcess, EventEmitter);\n   314→\n   315→\n   316→function flushStdio(subprocess) {\n   317→  const stdio = subprocess.stdio;\n   318→\n   319→  if (stdio == null) return;\n   320→\n   321→  for (let i = 0; i < stdio.length; i++) {\n   322→    const stream = stdio[i];\n   323→    // TODO(addaleax): This doesn't necessarily account for all the ways in\n   324→    // which data can be read from a stream, e.g. being consumed on the\n   325→    // native layer directly as a StreamBase.\n   326→    if (!stream || !stream.readable || stream[kIsUsedAsStdio]) {\n   327→      continue;\n   328→    }\n   329→ 339→function getHandleWrapType(stream) {\n   340→  if (stream instanceof Pipe) return 'pipe';\n   341→  if (stream instanceof TTY) return 'tty';\n   342→  if (stream instanceof TCP) return 'tcp';\n   343→  if (stream instanceof UDP) return 'udp';\n   344→\n   345→  return false;\n   346→}\n   347→\n   348→function closePendingHandle(target) {\n   349→  target._pendingMessage.handle.close();\n   350→  target._pendingMessage = null;\n   351→}\n   352→\n   353→\n   354→ChildProcess.prototype.spawn = function(options) {\n   355→  let i = 0;\n   356→\n   357→  validateObject(options, 370→                [undefined, 'json', 'advanced']);\n   371→  const serialization = options.serialization || 'json';\n   372→\n   373→  if (ipc !== undefined) {\n   374→    // Let child process know 394→\n   395→  const err = this._handle.spawn(options);\n   396→\n   397→  // Run-time errors should emit an error, not throw an exception.\n   398→  if (err === UV_EACCES ||\n   399→      err ===      return err;\n   409→  } else if (err) {\n   410→    // Close all opened fds on error\n   411→    for (i = 0; i < stdio.length; i++) {\n   412→      const stream = stdio[i];\n   413→      if (stream.type === 'pipe') {\n   414→        stream.handle.close();\n   415→      }\n   416→    }\n   417→\n   418→    this._handle.close();\n   419→    this._handle = null;\n   420→    throw new ErrnoException(err, 'spawn');\n   421→  } else {\n   422→    process.nextTick(onSpawnNT, this);\n   423→  }\n   424→\n   425→  this.pid = this._handle.pid;\n   426→\n   427→  for (i = 0; i < }\n   460→  }\n   461→\n   462→  this.stdin = stdio.length >= 1 && stdio[0].socket !== undefined ?\n   463→    stdio[0].socket : null;\n   464→  this.stdout = stdio.length >= 2 && stdio[1].socket !== 470→\n   471→  for (i = 0; i < stdio.length; i++)\n   472→    ArrayPrototypePush(this.stdio,\n   473→                       stdio[i].socket === undefined ? null : stdio[i].socket);\n   474→\n   475→  // Add .send() method and start listening for IPC data\n   476→  if (ipc !== undefined) setupChannel(this, ipc, serialization);\n   477→\n   478→  return err;\n   479→};\n   480→\n   481→\n   482→function onErrorNT(self, err) {\n   483→  self._handle.onexit(err);\n   484→}\n   485→\n   486→\n   487→function onSpawnNT(self) {\n   488→  self.emit('spawn');\n   489→}\n   490→\n   491→\n   492→ChildProcess.prototype.kill = function(sig) {\n   493→\n   494→  const signal = sig === 0 ? sig :\n   495→    convertToValidSignal(sig === undefined ? 'SIGTERM' : sig);\n   496→\n   497→  if (this._handle) {\n   498→    const err = this._handle.kill(signal);\n   499→    if (err === 0) {\n   500→      /* Success. */\n   501→      this.killed = true;\n   502→      return true;\n   503→    }\n   504→    if (err === UV_ESRCH) {\n   505→      /* Already dead. */\n   506→    } else if (err === UV_EINVAL || err === UV_ENOSYS) {\n   507→      /* The underlying platform doesn't support this signal. */\n   508→      throw new ErrnoException(err, 'kill');\n   509→    } else {\n   510→      /* Other error, almost certainly EPERM. */\n   511→      this.emit('error', new ErrnoException(err, 'kill'));\n   512→    }\n   513→  }\n   514→\n   515→  /* Kill didn't succeed. */\n   516→  return false;\n   517→};\n   518→\n   519→ChildProcess.prototype[SymbolDispose] = function() {\n   520→  if (!this.killed) {\n   521→    this.kill();\n   522→  }\n   523→};\n   524→\n   525→\n   526→ChildProcess.prototype.ref = function() {\n   527→  if (this._handle) this._handle.ref();\n   528→};\n   529→\n   530→\n   531→ChildProcess.prototype.unref = function() {\n   532→  if (this._handle) this._handle.unref();\n   533→};\n   534→\n   535→class Control extends EventEmitter {\n   536→  #channel = null;\n   537→  #refs = 0;\n   538→  #refExplicitlySet = false;\n   539→\n   540→  constructor(channel) {\n   541→    super();\n   542→    this.#channel = channel;\n   543→    this[kPendingMessages] = [];\n   544→  }\n   545→\n   546→  // The methods keeping track of the counter are being used to track the\n   547→  // listener count on the child process object as well as when writes are\n   548→  // in progress. Once the user has explicitly requested a certain state, these\n   549→  // methods become no-ops in order to not interfere with the user's intentions.\n   550→  refCounted() {\n   551→    if (++this.#refs === 1 && !this.#refExplicitlySet) {\n   552→      this.#channel.ref();\n   553→    }\n   554→  }\n   555→\n   556→  unrefCounted() {\n   557→    if (--this.#refs === 0 && !this.#refExplicitlySet) {\n   558→      this.#channel.unref();\n   559→      this.emit('unref');\n   560→    }\n   561→  }\n   562→\n   563→  ref() {\n   564→    this.#refExplicitlySet = true;\n   565→    this.#channel.ref();\n   566→  }\n   567→\n   568→  unref() {\n   569→    this.#refExplicitlySet = true;\n   570→    this.#channel.unref();\n   571→  }\n   572→\n   573→  get fd() {\n   574→    return this.#channel ? this.#channel.fd : undefined;\n   575→  }\n   576→}\n   577→\n   578→const channelDeprecationMsg = '_channel is deprecated. ' +\n   579→                              'Use ChildProcess.channel instead.';\n   580→\n   581→let serialization;\n   582→function setupChannel(target, channel, serializationMode) {\n   583→  const control = new Control(channel);\n   584→  target.channel = control;\n   585→  target[kChannelHandle] = channel;\n   586→\n   587→  ObjectDefineProperty(target, '_channel', {\n   588→    __proto__: null,\n   589→    get: deprecate(() => {\n   590→      return target.channel;\n   591→    }, channelDeprecationMsg, 'DEP0129'),\n   592→    set: deprecate((val) => {\n   593→      target.channel = val;\n   594→    }, channelDeprecationMsg, 'DEP0129'),\n   595→    configurable: true,\n   596→    enumerable: false,\n   597→  });\n   598→\n   599→  target._handleQueue = null;\n   600→  target._pendingMessage = null;\n   601→\n   602→  if (serialization === undefined)\n   603→    serialization = require('internal/child_process/serialization');\n   604→  const {\n   605→    initMessageChannel,\n   606→    parseChannelMessages,\n   607→    writeChannelMessage,\n   608→  } = serialization[serializationMode];\n   609→\n   610→  let pendingHandle = null;\n   611→  initMessageChannel(channel);\n   612→  channel.pendingHandle = null;\n   613→  channel.onread = function(arrayBuffer) {\n   614→    const recvHandle = channel.pendingHandle;\n   615→    channel.pendingHandle = null;\n   616→    if (arrayBuffer) {\n   617→      const nread = streamBaseState[kReadBytesOrError];\n   618→      const offset = streamBaseState[kArrayBufferOffset];\n   619→      const pool = new Uint8Array(arrayBuffer, offset, nread);\n   620→      if (recvHandle)\n   621→        pendingHandle = recvHandle;\n   622→\n   623→      for (const message of parseChannelMessages(channel, pool)) {\n   624→        // There will be at most one NODE_HANDLE message in every chunk we\n   625→        // read because SCM_RIGHTS messages don't get coalesced. Make sure\n   626→        // that we deliver the handle with the right message however.\n   627→        if (isInternal(message)) {\n   628→          if (message.cmd === 'NODE_HANDLE') {\n   629→            handleMessage(message, pendingHandle, true);\n   630→            pendingHandle = null;\n   631→          } else {\n   632→            handleMessage(message, undefined, true);\n   633→          }\n   634→        } else {\n   635→          handleMessage(message, undefined, false);\n   636→        }\n   637→      }\n   638→    } else {\n   639→      this.buffering = false;\n   640→      target.disconnect();\n   641→      channel.onread = nop;\n   642→      channel.close();\n   643→      target.channel = null;\n   644→      maybeClose(target);\n   645→    }\n   646→  };\n   647→\n   648→  // Object where socket lists will live\n   649→  channel.sockets = { got: {}, send: {} };\n   650→\n   651→  // Handlers will go through this\n   652→  target.on('internalMessage', function(message, handle) {\n   653→    // Once acknowledged - continue sending handles.\n   654→    if (message.cmd === 'NODE_HANDLE_ACK' ||\n   655→        message.cmd === 'NODE_HANDLE_NACK') {\n   656→\n   657→      if (target._pendingMessage) {\n   658→        if (message.cmd === 'NODE_HANDLE_ACK') {\n   659→          closePendingHandle(target);\n   660→        } else if (target._pendingMessage.retransmissions++ ===\n   661→                   MAX_HANDLE_RETRANSMISSIONS) {\n   662→          closePendingHandle(target);\n   663→          process.emitWarning('Handle did not reach the receiving process ' +\n   664→                              'correctly', 'SentHandleNotReceivedWarning');\n   665→        }\n   666→      }\n   667→\n   668→      assert(ArrayIsArray(target._handleQueue));\n   669→      const queue = target._handleQueue;\n   670→      target._handleQueue = null;\n   671→\n   672→      if (target._pendingMessage) {\n   673→        target._send(target._pendingMessage.message,\n   674→                     target._pendingMessage.handle,\n   675→                     target._pendingMessage.options,\n   676→                     target._pendingMessage.callback);\n   677→      }\n   678→\n   679→      for (let i = 0; i < queue.length; i++) {\n   680→        const args = queue[i];\n   681→        target._send(args.message, args.handle, args.options, args.callback);\n   682→      }\n   683→\n   684→      // Process a pending disconnect (if any).\n   685→      if (!target.connected && target.channel && !target._handleQueue)\n   686→        target._disconnect();\n   687→\n   688→      return;\n   689→    }\n   690→\n   691→    if (message.cmd !== 'NODE_HANDLE') return;\n   692→\n   693→    // It is possible that the handle is not received because of some error on\n   694→    // ancillary data reception such as MSG_CTRUNC. In this case, report the\n   695→    // sender about it by sending a NODE_HANDLE_NACK message.\n   696→    if (!handle)\n   697→      return target._send({ cmd: 'NODE_HANDLE_NACK' }, null, true);\n   698→\n   699→    // Acknowledge handle receival. Don't emit error events (for example if\n   700→    // the other side has disconnected) because this call to send() is not\n   701→    // initiated by the user and it shouldn't be fatal to be unable to ACK\n   702→    // a message.\n   703→    target._send({ cmd: 'NODE_HANDLE_ACK' }, null, true);\n   704→\n   705→    const obj = handleConversion[message.type];\n   706→\n   707→    // Update    ReflectApply(target.emit, target, messages[i]);\n   730→      }\n   731→\n   732→      target.channel[kPendingMessages] = [];\n   733→    });\n   734→  });\n   735→\n   736→  target.send = function(message, handle, options, callback) {\n   737→    if (typeof handle === 'function') {\n   738→      callback = handle;\n   739→      handle = undefined;\n   740→      options = undefined;\n   741→    } else if (typeof options === 'function') {\n   742→      callback = options;\n   743→      options = undefined;\n   744→    } else if (options !== undefined) {\n   745→      validateObject(options, 'options');\n   746→    }\n   747→\n   748→    options = { swallowErrors: false, ...options };\n   749→\n   750→    if (this.connected) {\n   751→      return process.nextTick(callback, ex);\n   756→    } else {\n   757→      process.nextTick(() => this.emit('error', ex));\n   758→    }\n   759→    return false;\n   760→  };\n   761→\n   762→  target._send = function(message, handle, options, callback) {\n   763→    assert(this.connected || this.channel);\n   764→\n   765→    if (message === undefined)\n   766→      throw new ERR_MISSING_ARGS('message');\n   767→\n   768→    // Non-serializable messages should not reach the remote\n   769→    // end point; as any failure in the stringification there\n   770→    // will result in error message that is weakly consumable.\n   771→    // So perform a final check on message prior to sending.\n   772→    if (typeof message !== 'string' &&\n   773→        typeof message !== 'object' &&\n   774→        typeof message !== 'number' &&\n   775→        typeof message !== 'boolean') {\n   776→      throw new ERR_INVALID_ARG_TYPE(\n   777→        'message', ['string', 'object', 'number', 'boolean'], message);\n   778→    }\n   779→\n   780→    // Support legacy function signature\n   781→    if (typeof options === 'boolean') {\n   782→      options = { swallowErrors: options };\n   783→    }\n   784→\n   785→    let obj;\n   786→\n   787→    // Package messages with a handle object\n   788→    if (handle) {\n   789→      // This message will be handled by an internalMessage event handler\n   790→      message = {\n   791→        cmd: 'NODE_HANDLE',\n   792→        type: null,\n   793→        msg: message,\n   794→      };\n   795→\n   796→      if (handle instanceof net.Socket) {\n   797→        message.type = 'net.Socket';\n   798→      } else if (handle instanceof net.Server) {\n   799→        message.type = 'net.Server';\n   800→      } else if (handle instanceof TCP || handle instanceof Pipe) {\n   801→        message.type = 'net.Native';\n   802→      } else if (handle instanceof dgram.Socket) {\n   803→        message.type = 'dgram.Socket';\n   804→      } else if (handle instanceof UDP) {\n   805→        message.type = 'dgram.Native';\n   806→      } else {\n   807→        throw new ERR_INVALID_HANDLE_TYPE();\n   808→      }\n   809→\n   810→      // Queue-up message and handle if we haven't received ACK yet.\n   811→      if (this._handleQueue) {\n   812→        ArrayPrototypePush(this._handleQueue, {\n   813→          callback: callback,\n   814→          handle: handle,\n   815→          options: options,\n   816→          message: message.msg,\n   817→        });\n   818→        return this._handleQueue.length === 1;\n   819→      }\n   820→\n   821→      obj = handleConversion[message.type];\n   822→\n   823→      // convert TCP object to native handle object\n   824→      handle =
